=== Iteration 1 - [2025-08-30 21:14:30] ===
PLAN:
  ### Adjusted Environment Setup Plan
  #### **Key Adjustments Based on Hardware (Linux/amd64)**
  - Removed all **Windows-specific components** (Visual C++, `less`, Scoop/Choco, paths like `%APPDATA%`).
  - Replaced Windows package managers with **Linux-native methods** (APT).
  - Omitted **GPU/CUDA dependencies** (none were present).
  - Simplified paths using **Linux conventions** (`~/.config`, `/etc/bat`).
  - Excluded **cross-platform tests** irrelevant to Linux (Cygwin, Windows paths).
  - Added **Docker-in-Docker (DinD)** setup for containerized benchmarks.
  - Optimized storage via multi-stage Docker builds.
  ---

  - **Docker CE CLI** (benchmarks)

  - **CI/CD & Docs**:

    - Pager behavior (`less -RF`)

  ---
  ### 4. COMPLETE TODO LIST (Linux/amd64 Focus)
  ```bash
  # INSTALLATIONS (APT)
  sudo apt update
  sudo apt install -y bat git fzf ripgrep fd jq dpkg fakeroot iconv
  cargo install cargo-audit cross bat-extras
  # DOCKER SETUP (DinD for benchmarks)
  curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | sh
  sudo usermod -aG docker $USER  # Enable non-root access
  # CONFIGURATION
  mkdir -p ~/.config/bat
  echo '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > ~/.config/bat/config
  sudo mkdir -p /etc/bat
  sudo cp ~/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config  # System-wide defaults
  # ENVIRONMENT VARIABLES (persistent)
  echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> ~/.bashrc
  echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> ~/.bashrc
  source ~/.bashrc
  # PROJECT SETUP
  git submodule update --init --recursive
  bat cache --build  # Verify themes/languages: bat --list-themes
  # DOCKER IMAGE BUILD (benchmarks)
  cd tests/benchmarks/startup-time-src
  docker build -t bat-benchmark .
  docker run --rm bat-benchmark
  docker rmi bat-benchmark
  # VERIFICATIONS
  bat --version  # ≥0.25.0
  cargo audit --version
  docker --version
  bat README.md  # Core functionality
  fzf --preview "bat --color=always {}"  # Integration
  ```
  ---
  ### Hardware-Specific Notes:
  1. **Storage Optimization**: Use multi-stage Docker builds to minimize image size.
  2. **Paths**: All configs use Linux defaults (`~/.config`, `/etc`).
  3. **CPU**: Tests assume `amd64` architecture; ARM cross-compilation via `cross`.
  4. **GPU**: No GPU dependencies—benchmarks are CPU-only.
NEXT:
  current progress
  The Dockerfile uses a multi-stage build to install bat, bat-extras, Rust tools, and runtime dependencies. The build failed at the runtime dependencies installation step due to an error when installing packages via apt-get, specifically while attempting to install docker.io. The Dockerfile structure includes proper configuration setup, environment variables, and user configuration but contains unnecessary Docker-related components in the runtime stage.
  next step
  Remove docker.io installation from the runtime stage's apt-get command and eliminate the usermod docker group assignment since Docker-in-Docker setup is only required for host-level benchmarks.

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.73-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install build dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y wget dpkg fakeroot git clang cmake libiconv-dev pkg-config libssl-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-audit cross
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq dpkg fakeroot iconv less docker.io && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user and configure Docker access
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user && \
      usermod -aG docker user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 1 ---

  ```dockerfile
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.73-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install build dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y wget dpkg fakeroot git clang cmake libiconv-dev pkg-config libssl-dev && \

  # Install bat-extras

      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \

      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-audit cross
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq dpkg fakeroot iconv less && \

  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
  ```
  Key changes made:
  1. Removed `docker.io` from the runtime dependencies installation
  2. Removed the `usermod` command that added user to docker group
  3. Kept all other functionality intact including bat configuration setup

  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.73-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install build dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y wget dp极速下载kg fakeroot git clang cmake libiconv-dev pkg-config libssl-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-audit cross
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq dpkg fakeroot iconv less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.73-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install build dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y wget dpkg fakeroot git clang cmake libiconv-dev pkg-config libssl-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-audit cross
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq dpkg fakeroot less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 4 ---

  ### 4. COMPLETE TODO LIST (Linux/amd64 Focus)
  ```bash
  # INSTALLATIONS (APT)
  sudo apt update
  sudo apt install -y bat git fzf ripgrep fd jq dpkg fakeroot iconv
  cargo install cargo-audit cross bat-extras
  # DOCKER SETUP (DinD for benchmarks)
  curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | sh
  sudo usermod -aG docker $USER  # Enable non-root access
  # CONFIGURATION
  mkdir -p ~/.config/bat
  echo '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > ~/.config/bat/config
  sudo mkdir -p /etc/bat
  sudo cp ~/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config  # System-wide defaults
  # ENVIRONMENT VARIABLES (persistent)
  echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> ~/.bashrc
  echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> ~/.bashrc
  source ~/.bashrc
  # PROJECT SETUP
  git submodule update --init --recursive
  bat cache --build  # Verify themes/languages: bat --list-themes
  # DOCKER IMAGE BUILD (benchmarks)
  cd tests/benchmarks/startup-time-src
  docker build -t bat-benchmark .
  docker run --rm bat-benchmark
  docker rmi bat-benchmark
  # VERIFICATIONS
  bat --version  # ≥0.25.0
  cargo audit --version
  docker --version
  bat README.md  # Core functionality
  fzf --preview "bat --color=always {}"  # Integration
  ```

  1. **Storage Optimization**: Use multi-stage Docker builds to minimize image size.

  Runtime Status: Failed
  Runtime Output:
  Runtime Error:
  === Execution End ===
DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.73-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install build dependencies and tools with retry mechanism
  RUN apt-get update || apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget dpkg fakeroot git clang cmake libiconv-dev pkg-config libssl-dev \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-audit cross
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq dpkg fakeroot less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ```bash
  sudo apt update
  sudo apt install -y bat git fzf ripgrep fd jq dpkg fakeroot iconv
  cargo install cargo-audit cross bat-extras

  docker --version
  bat README.md  # Core functionality
  fzf --preview "bat --color=always {}"  # Integration
  ```

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.73-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install build dependencies and tools
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget dpkg fakeroot git clang cmake libiconv-dev pkg-config libssl-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-audit cross
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq dpkg fakeroot less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.73-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Update package lists first
  RUN apt-get update
  # Install essential dependencies individually to isolate issues
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends wget
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends dpkg
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends fakeroot
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends git
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends clang
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends cmake
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends pkg-config
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends libssl-dev
  RUN apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends libc6-dev
  RUN rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-audit cross
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 8 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.73-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools with verbose logging
  RUN cargo install -v cargo-audit
  RUN cargo install -v cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.77-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools with verbose logging in single command
  RUN cargo install -v cargo-audit cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ### 4. COMPLETE TODO LIST (Linux/amd64 Focus)
  ```bash
  # INSTALLATIONS (APT)
  sudo apt update
  sudo apt install -y bat git fzf ripgrep fd jq dpkg fakeroot iconv
  cargo install cargo-audit cross bat-extras
  # DOCKER SETUP (DinD for benchmarks)
  curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | sh
  sudo usermod -aG docker $USER  # Enable non-root access
  # CONFIGURATION
  mkdir -p ~/.config/bat
  echo '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > ~/.config/bat/config
  sudo mkdir -p /etc/bat
  sudo cp ~/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config  # System-wide defaults
  # ENVIRONMENT VARIABLES (persistent)
  echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> ~/.bashrc
  echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> ~/.bashrc
  source ~/.bashrc
  # PROJECT SETUP
  git submodule update --init --recursive
  bat cache --build  # Verify themes/languages: bat --list-themes
  # DOCKER IMAGE BUILD (benchmarks)
  cd tests/benchmarks/startup-time-src
  docker build -t bat-benchmark .
  docker run --rm bat-benchmark
  docker rmi bat-benchmark
  # VERIFICATIONS
  bat --version  # ≥0.25.0
  cargo audit --version
  docker --version
  bat README.md  # Core functionality
  fzf --preview "bat --color=always {}"  # Integration
  ```

  1. **Storage Optimization**: Use multi-stage Docker builds to minimize image size.
  2. **Paths**: All configs use Linux defaults (`~/.config`, `/etc`).
  3. **CPU**: Tests assume `amd64` architecture; ARM cross-compilation via `cross`.
  4. **GPU**: No GPU dependencies—benchmarks are CPU-only.

  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.77-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools in separate commands
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y cargo-audit && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN cargo install -v cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.77-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools using cargo
  RUN cargo install -v cargo-audit cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ```bash
  # INSTALLATIONS (APT)
  sudo apt update
  sudo apt install -y bat git fzf ripgrep fd jq dpkg fakeroot iconv

  # DOCKER SETUP (DinD for benchmarks)

  # CONFIGURATION

  sudo mkdir -p /etc/bat

  source ~/.bashrc
  # PROJECT SETUP
  git submodule update --init --recursive
  bat cache --build  # Verify themes/languages: bat --list-themes
  # DOCKER IMAGE BUILD (benchmarks)
  cd tests/benchmarks/startup-time-src
  docker build -t bat-benchmark .
  docker run --rm bat-benchmark
  docker rmi bat-benchmark
  # VERIFICATIONS
  bat --version  # ≥0.25.0
  cargo audit --version
  docker --version
  bat README.md  # Core functionality
  fzf --preview "bat --color=always {}"  # Integration
  ```

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.77-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential \
          libdbus-1-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Install Rust tools using cargo
  RUN cargo install -v cargo-audit
  RUN cargo install -v cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 14 ---

  ### 4. COMPLETE TODO LIST (Linux/amd64 Focus)
  ```bash
  # INSTALLATIONS (APT)
  sudo apt update
  sudo apt install -y bat git fzf ripgrep fd jq dpkg fakeroot iconv
  cargo install cargo-audit cross bat-extras
  # DOCKER SETUP (DinD for benchmarks)
  curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | sh
  sudo usermod -aG docker $USER  # Enable non-root access
  # CONFIGURATION
  mkdir -p ~/.config/bat
  echo '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > ~/.config/bat/config
  sudo mkdir -p /etc/bat
  sudo cp ~/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config  # System-wide defaults
  # ENVIRONMENT VARIABLES (persistent)
  echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> ~/.bashrc
  echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> ~/.bashrc
  source ~/.bashrc
  # PROJECT SETUP
  git submodule update --init --recursive
  bat cache --build  # Verify themes/languages: bat --list-themes
  # DOCKER IMAGE BUILD (benchmarks)
  cd tests/benchmarks/startup-time-src
  docker build -t bat-benchmark .
  docker run --rm bat-benchmark
  docker rmi bat-benchmark
  # VERIFICATIONS
  bat --version  # ≥0.25.0
  cargo audit --version
  docker --version
  bat README.md  # Core functionality
  fzf --preview "bat --color=always {}"  # Integration
  ```
  ---
  ### Hardware-Specific Notes:
  1. **Storage Optimization**: Use multi-stage Docker builds to minimize image size.
  2. **Paths**: All configs use Linux defaults (`~/.config`, `/etc`).
  3. **CPU**: Tests assume `amd64` architecture; ARM cross-compilation via `cross`.
  4. **GPU**: No GPU dependencies—benchmarks are CPU-only.

DOCKERFILE:
  Based on the failure log and recommendations, here's the modified Dockerfile:
  ```dockerfile
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.77-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential \
          libdbus-1-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_极.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Update Rust toolchain before installing tools
  RUN rustup update stable
  # Install Rust tools using cargo
  RUN cargo install -v cargo-audit --features vendored
  RUN cargo install -v cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
  ```

  FROM rust:1.77-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential \
          libdbus-1-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          libgit2-dev \
          libssh2-1-dev && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Update Rust toolchain before installing tools
  RUN rustup update stable
  # Install Rust tools using cargo
  RUN cargo install -v cargo-audit --features vendored
  RUN cargo install -v cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''col -bx | bat -l man -p'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN git submodule update --init --recursive && \
      bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 18 ---

  ```bash
  # INSTALLATIONS (APT)
  sudo apt update

  # DOCKER SETUP (DinD for benchmarks)

  # CONFIGURATION

  echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> ~/.bashrc
  source ~/.bashrc
  # PROJECT SETUP
  git submodule update --init --recursive
  bat cache --build  # Verify themes/languages: bat --list-themes
  # DOCKER IMAGE BUILD (benchmarks)
  cd tests/benchmarks/startup-time-src
  docker build -t bat-benchmark .
  docker run --rm bat-benchmark
  docker rmi bat-benchmark
  # VERIFICATIONS
  bat --version  # ≥0.25.0
  cargo audit --version
  docker --version
  bat README.md  # Core functionality
  fzf --preview "bat --color=always {}"  # Integration
  ```

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.77-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer including perl
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential \
          libdbus-1-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          libgit2-dev \
          libssh2-1-dev \
          perl && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Update Rust toolchain before installing tools
  RUN rustup update stable
  # Install Rust tools using cargo without vendored feature
  RUN cargo install -v cargo-audit cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''col -bx | bat -l man -p'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  ### 4. COMPLETE TODO LIST (Linux/amd64 Focus)
  ```bash
  # INSTALLATIONS (APT)
  sudo apt update
  sudo apt install -y bat git fzf ripgrep fd jq dpkg fakeroot iconv
  cargo install cargo-audit cross bat-extras
  # DOCKER SETUP (DinD for benchmarks)
  curl -fsSL https://get.docker.com | sh
  sudo usermod -aG docker $USER  # Enable non-root access
  # CONFIGURATION
  mkdir -p ~/.config/bat
  echo '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > ~/.config/bat/config
  sudo mkdir -p /etc/bat
  sudo cp ~/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config  # System-wide defaults
  # ENVIRONMENT VARIABLES (persistent)
  echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> ~/.bashrc
  echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''awk \"{ gsub(/\\x1B\\[[0-9;]*m/, \"\", \$0); gsub(/.\\x08/, \"\", \$0); print }\" | bat -p -lman'\''"' >> ~/.bashrc
  source ~/.bashrc
  # PROJECT SETUP
  git submodule update --init --recursive
  bat cache --build  # Verify themes/languages: bat --list-themes
  # DOCKER IMAGE BUILD (benchmarks)
  cd tests/benchmarks/startup-time-src
  docker build -t bat-benchmark .
  docker run --rm bat-benchmark
  docker rmi bat-benchmark
  # VERIFICATIONS
  bat --version  # ≥0.25.0
  cargo audit --version
  docker --version
  bat README.md  # Core functionality
  fzf --preview "bat --color=always {}"  # Integration
  ```

  ### Hardware-Specific Notes:
  1. **Storage Optimization**: Use multi-stage Docker builds to minimize image size.
  2. **Paths**: All configs use Linux defaults (`~/.config`, `/etc`).
  3. **CPU**: Tests assume `amd64` architecture; ARM cross-compilation via `cross`.
  4. **GPU**: No GPU dependencies—benchmarks are CPU-only.

DOCKERFILE:
  # Stage 1: Build stage for tools and dependencies
  FROM rust:1.77-slim-bullseye AS builder
  # Install all build dependencies in a single layer including perl
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          wget \
          dpkg \
          fakeroot \
          git \
          clang \
          cmake \
          pkg-config \
          libssl-dev \
          libc6-dev \
          build-essential \
          libdbus-1-dev \
          libsqlite3-dev \
          libgit2-dev \
          libssh2-1-dev \
          perl && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install bat from GitHub release
  RUN wget https://github.com/sharkdp/bat/releases/download/v0.25.0/bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      dpkg -i bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb && \
      rm bat_0.25.0_amd64.deb
  # Install bat-extras
  RUN git clone https://github.com/eth-p/bat-extras.git /tmp/bat-extras && \
      cd /tmp/bat-extras && \
      ./build.sh --install && \
      cd / && \
      rm -rf /tmp/bat-extras
  # Update Rust toolchain before installing tools
  RUN rustup update stable
  # Install Rust tools using cargo with verbose logging and separate commands
  RUN cargo install --verbose cargo-audit
  RUN cargo install --verbose cross
  # Clean cargo cache to reduce layer size
  RUN rm -rf /usr/local/cargo/registry/*
  # Stage 2: Final runtime image
  FROM debian:bullseye-slim
  # Install runtime dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y git fzf ripgrep fd-find jq less && \
      ln -s /usr/bin/fdfind /usr/bin/fd && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Copy installed binaries from builder
  COPY --from=builder /usr/bin/bat /usr/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/bin/bat* /usr/local/bin/
  COPY --from=builder /usr/local/cargo/bin/cargo-audit /usr/local/cargo/bin/cross /usr/local/bin/
  # Create user
  RUN groupadd -r user && useradd -r -g user user
  # Set up bat configuration
  RUN mkdir -p /home/user/.config/bat && \
      echo -e '--theme="TwoDark"\n--style="numbers,changes,header"\n--italic-text=always\n--pager="less -RF"' > /home/user/.config/bat/config && \
      mkdir -p /etc/bat && \
      cp /home/user/.config/bat/config /etc/bat/config
  # Set environment variables
  RUN echo 'export BAT_PAGER="less -RFK"' >> /home/user/.bashrc && \
      echo 'export MANPAGER="sh -c '\''col -bx | bat -l man -p'\''"' >> /home/user/.bashrc
  # Copy repository content
  COPY . /app
  WORKDIR /app
  # Final setup steps
  USER user
  RUN bat cache --build
  # Default command
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
